<body lang=ZH-TW style='tab-interval:24.0pt;text-justify-trim:punctuation'>

<div class=WordSection1 style='layout-grid:18.0pt'>

<p class=MsoNormal><span class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>Airbyte</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>
is an open-source platform that facilitates data integration and replication.
It simplifies the process of collecting and moving data from various sources to
data warehouses or other destinations. With a focus on ease of use and
extensibility, <span class=SpellE>Airbyte</span> enables organizations to build
robust data pipelines and ensure reliable data synchronization across different
systems.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:37.5pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
7.5pt;margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:13.5pt;font-family:
"Arial","sans-serif";color:#3775A4'>Requirements <o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:.5pt'><span class=SpellE><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>Kubernetes</span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>
1.25+ or Rancher 2.7.3+<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:37.5pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
7.5pt;margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:13.5pt;font-family:
"Arial","sans-serif";color:#3775A4'>Prerequisites</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:24.5pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
Arial;color:#666666'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>At least one storage class has
been created.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:24.5pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-24.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";mso-fareast-font-family:
Arial;color:#666666'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>At least one persistent volume
claim has been created.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<table class=ab border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style='border-collapse:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:37.5pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
7.5pt;margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:13.5pt;font-family:
"Arial","sans-serif";color:#3775A4'>How to Deploy<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:6.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>Click <b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Install</b>. During the installing
procedure, you can check and configure the parameters. If you want to set
advanced settings, click <b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>Edit YAML</b>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:22.5pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
7.5pt;margin-left:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>Service<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:15.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>For the
app image service type, you can expose <span class=SpellE>Airbyte</span> to the
Internet and provide an external access. There are two options for you to
choose: <span class=SpellE>LoadBalancer</span> and <span class=SpellE>NodePort</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
7.5pt;margin-left:23.8pt;mso-para-margin-top:0cm;mso-para-margin-right:0cm;
mso-para-margin-bottom:7.5pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;text-indent:-24.1pt;
mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:#666666'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>l<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:#666666'>LoadBalancer</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>: Configure a load
balancer IP from the VIP (Virtual IP) address pool. This IP will be used to
route external traffic to <span class=SpellE>Airbyte</span>.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:23.8pt;mso-para-margin-left:0gd;
text-indent:-24.1pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo4'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:
Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings;color:#666666'><span style='mso-list:
Ignore'>l<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
class=SpellE><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
color:#666666'>NodePort</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.5pt;
font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>: Configure a specific port
number. If no port is configured, a random port will be assigned automatically.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-top:22.5pt;margin-right:0cm;margin-bottom:
7.5pt;margin-left:0cm'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='mso-bidi-font-size:12.0pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif"'>Advanced
Setting<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:15.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";color:#666666'>The
following table lists the configurable parameters of the <span class=SpellE>Airbyte</span>
chart and their default values.<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-bottom:7.5pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Arial","sans-serif";
mso-themecolor:text1'>Configuration parameters<o:p></o:p></span></p>
